 It is advisable to eat cold in summer

 isse andruni thandak bani rahati he or is lihaaj se dahi kaaphi phydemand he
 Eating yogurt in summer keeps the body temperature balanced
 iske alaava ye pachan kriya ke liye bhi bahut phydemand he
 The calcium, protein and many other nutrients present in yogurt are helpful in fulfilling many needs of the body
 lekin har cheez kii tarah dahi khaane ke bhi kuch khaas niyam hote hai

 64parkaarobaar kar rahaa he jabaki nifti main kareeb 100 ank upar 10903 par kaarobaar karne laga
 Explain that the Bombay Stock Exchange's Sensex lost 21 points to 35,556, losing 21 points on Monday
 71 ank par band hua tha
 Investors took a cautious stand before the results of the Karnataka Assembly elections
 brokaron ne kaha tha ki vrihad aarthik aankadon kaa bhi aakarshan bazaar main nahin dekha gaya
 Karnataka election results will come today
 zyaadaatar agsit nateezon main sattadhari congress or bhaajapa ke bich kadaa sangharsh hone kii sambhaavna jataai gai he
 Meanwhile, wpi-based inflation rose to 3 in April
 18 pratishat par pahunch gai
 At the same time, the industrial production growth rate of the month of March decreased to a five-month low of 4
 4 pratishat par aa gai he
 Its figures came after the market closed on Friday

 However, the Sensex finally ended with a series of profit-booking in between

 But are they as safe as fds
 nishchit rup se nahin
 Debt funds are less volatile than equity funds, yet they do not guarantee fixed returns like fds
 darasal unamem do tarah ke jokhim hote hai—credit jokhim or byaaj dar kaa jokhim
 What does this mean for your investment? credit jokhimaiskaa sambandh company kii ore se byaaj ke jokhim yaa mul bhugtan karne main aakshamata se hota he
 Recently, some debt papers have shown losses due to the fall in the value of debt papers of these companies after the ratings of some companies like IL&FS and DHFL
 ielandeeyes kii group companiyon kii ore se byaaj ke bhugtan main difolt hona or reating agenciyon kii ore se dchaefeel ke patron kii reating giraane ke kaaran inamen jin mutual funds ne nivesh kiya tha, unki shuddh sampattiyon (net esets) ke mulyon main giravat aa gai thi
 The performance of a fund depends on the fund manager's ability to take credit risk
 apekshaakrit nimna-reating vaale patr ooncha byaaj dene kii peshkash karte hai or jaahir he isse milane vaala laabh bhi adhik hota he lekin inamen jokhim bhi zyada hota he
 Mahendra Jajoo, head of fixed income at Mirae Asset AMC, says, "investors should not panic in such cases but analyze the situation carefully
" pehle ho chuke nuksaan par dhyaan dene ke bajaae unhen credit or bazaar kii sthiti samet sabhi jaankariyon ke aadhaar par nuksaan kii sambhaavna or seemaa kaa akalan karnaa chahie
 "interest rate risk" is the inverse relationship between the price of the letter of credit and the interest rates
 unki keemten—or funds ke enevi—byaaj daron main badhotaree ke saath gir jaati hai or byaaj daron main giravat ke saath bad jaati hai
 Reducing the Risk Despite the risk, letter of credit is beneficial from the income tax point of view as it attracts a tax of 20 per cent after three years of profit whereas on the benefit from FD, the investor has to pay tax according to the income slab which is relatively Is greater
 rin patron kii nishchit rup se andekhi nahin kii ja sakati, khaskar unke liye jo tex kii oonchi shrenee ke daayre main aate hai
 Therefore, it is very important to choose the right category of funds
 sebi ne rin patron ko unki avadhi or credit quality (dekhen graphics) ke aadhaar par kai shreniyon main vargeekrut kar diya he taaki niveshak lakshya ke anusaar koshon kaa chunaav kar saken
 "investors should invest in debt papers that have an effective maturity close to the investment period," says Nirav Karkera, head of research at Myway Wealth
 '' iske alaava, jo log jokhim lene se darate hai, unhen portpholio kii quality se kisi tarah kaa samjhauta nahin karnaa chahie
 Nitin Shanbag, Senior Group Vice President, Investment Products, Motilal Oswal Private Wealth Management, says that to avoid immediate backlash, the investor should carefully review the portfolio of the letter of credit to ascertain the risk
